        <div class="col-xs-12 download_metrics_data">
          Download the metrics data: 
         <a href="https://s3.amazonaws.com/bsp-ocsit-prod-east-appdata/datagov/wordpress/agency-participation.csv" class="external ext-link" rel="external" onclick="this.target='_blank';"> [CSV] </a> | 
         <a href="https://s3.amazonaws.com/bsp-ocsit-prod-east-appdata/datagov/wordpress/agency-participation.xlsx" class="external ext-link" rel="external" onclick="this.target='_blank';"> [EXCEL] </a>

       <div class="row"> 
        <div class="col-xs-12"> 
         <p style="text-align: left; clear: both;">Data.gov captures a variety of metrics on the participation of the agencies that supply datasets to Data.gov. The <a href="http://labs.data.gov/dashboard/offices" class="local-link">Project Open Data Dashboard</a> provides detailed information on how federal agencies are implementing the <a href="https://project-open-data.cio.gov/policy-memo/" class="external ext-link" rel="external" onclick="this.target='_blank';">Federal Open Data Policy</a></p> 
         <p style="text-align: left; clear: both;">Visitor metrics on the number of views for specific datasets is available as a <a href="//catalog.data.gov/dataset/data-gov-visitor-metrics" class="local-link">dataset</a></p> 
         <p>Below are the details on the dataset counts by participating agencies and their component sub-agencies. </p> 
         <div style="display: block !important; margin:0 !important; padding: 0 !important" id="wpp_popup_post_end_element"></div> 
        </div> 
       </div>

      <script type="text/javascript">
    jQuery(function ($) {
        $('.agencyExpand').on('click', function () {
            $('.' + $(this).parent().attr('rel')).show('slow');
            $(this).parent().children('.agencyHide').show();
            $(this).hide();
        });
        $('.agencyHide').on('click', function () {
            $('.' + $(this).parent().attr('rel')).hide('slow');
            $(this).parent().children('.agencyExpand').show();
            $(this).hide();
        });
        $('.more-link').each(function () {
            var rel = $(this).attr('rel');
            if ($('.sub-agency.' + rel).size() < 2) {
                $(this).remove()
            }
        });
        $('.agencies_total_count').html($('tr.sub-agency a.sub-agency').size() + $('tr.parent-agency').size());
        $('.publishers_total_count').html($('tr.sub-agency a.publisher').size());
        $('.total_dataset_count').html('230,639');
        $('#total_dataset_sum').html("266,365");
                    $(".Federal-Government").click(function() {
                $("html,body").animate({
                    scrollTop: $(".Federal-Government_scroll").offset().top}, 'medium');
            });            $(".Other-Federal").click(function() {
                $("html,body").animate({
                    scrollTop: $(".Other-Federal_scroll").offset().top}, 'medium');
            });            $(".City-Government").click(function() {

                    scrollTop: $(".City-Government_scroll").offset().top}, 'medium');
            });            $(".Cooperative").click(function() {

            });            $(".County-Government").click(function() {

            });            $(".Non-Profit").click(function() {
